Inkscape's primary vector graphics format is Scalable Vector Graphics (SVG), however many other formats can be imported and exported.\r\n\r\nInkscape can render primitive vector shapes (e.g. rectangles, ellipses, polygons, arcs, spirals, stars and 3D boxes) and text.
